  ‚éŅ ¬†Added 272 lines
      150      }
      151  }
      152  
      153 +/// Coerce an object to a matrix.                             
      154 +///                                                           
      155 +/// For vectors, creates a single-column matrix. For data fram
          +es, converts                                                  
      156 +/// all columns to a common type and combines into a matrix.  
      157 +///                                                           
      158 +/// @param x object to coerce                                 
      159 +/// @return matrix (vector with dim attribute)                
      160 +/// @namespace base                                           
      161 +#[builtin(name = "as.matrix", min_args = 1)]                  
      162 +fn builtin_as_matrix(args: &[RValue], _: &[(String, RValue)]) 
          +-> Result<RValue, RError> {                                   
      163 +    match args.first() {                                      
      164 +        Some(RValue::Vector(v)) => {                          
      165 +            let len = v.len();                                
      166 +            let mut rv = v.clone();                           
      167 +            rv.set_attr(                                      
      168 +                "dim".to_string(),                            
      169 +                RValue::vec(Vector::Integer(vec![Some(len as i
          +64), Some(1)].into())),                                       
      170 +            );                                                
      171 +            Ok(RValue::Vector(rv))                            
      172 +        }                                                     
      173 +        Some(RValue::List(list)) => {                         
      174 +            // Data frame ‚Üí matrix: convert all columns to dou
          +ble, combine column-major                                     
      175 +            let ncol = list.values.len();                     
      176 +            if ncol == 0 {                                    
      177 +                return Ok(RValue::vec(Vector::Double(vec![].in
          +to())));                                                      
      178 +            }                                                 
      179 +            let nrow = list                                   
      180 +                .values                                       
      181 +                .first()                                      
      182 +                .map(|(_, v)| match v {                       
      183 +                    RValue::Vector(rv) => rv.len(),           
      184 +                    _ => 1,                                   
      185 +                })                                            
      186 +                .unwrap_or(0);                                
      187 +                                                              
      188 +            let mut data: Vec<Option<f64>> = Vec::with_capacit
          +y(nrow * ncol);                                               
      189 +            for (_, val) in &list.values {                    
      190 +                if let Some(v) = val.as_vector() {            
      191 +                    let doubles = v.to_doubles();             
      192 +                    data.extend(&doubles);                    
      193 +                } else {                                      
      194 +                    for _ in 0..nrow {                        
      195 +                        data.push(None);                      
      196 +                    }                                         
      197 +                }                                             
      198 +            }                                                 
      199 +            let mut rv = RVector::from(Vector::Double(data.int
          +o()));                                                        
      200 +            rv.set_attr(                                      
      201 +                "dim".to_string(),                            
      202 +                RValue::vec(Vector::Integer(                  
      203 +                    vec![Some(nrow as i64), Some(ncol as i64)]
          +.into(),                                                      
      204 +                )),                                           
      205 +            );                                                
      206 +            // Copy column names as dimnames                  
      207 +            let col_names: Vec<Option<String>> =              
      208 +                list.values.iter().map(|(n, _)| n.clone()).col
          +lect();                                                       
      209 +            if col_names.iter().any(|n| n.is_some()) {        
      210 +                let dimnames = RValue::List(RList::new(vec![  
      211 +                    (None, RValue::Null),                     
      212 +                    (                                         
      213 +                        None,                                 
      214 +                        RValue::vec(Vector::Character(col_name
          +s.into())),                                                   
      215 +                    ),                                        
      216 +                ]));                                          
      217 +                rv.set_attr("dimnames".to_string(), dimnames);
      218 +            }                                                 
      219 +            Ok(RValue::Vector(rv))                            
      220 +        }                                                     
      221 +        Some(RValue::Null) => Ok(RValue::vec(Vector::Double(ve
          +c![].into()))),                                               
      222 +        _ => Ok(RValue::vec(Vector::Double(vec![None].into()))
          +),                                                            
      223 +    }                                                         
      224 +}                                                             
      225 +                                                              
      226 +/// Coerce an object to a data frame.                         
      227 +///                                                           
      228 +/// @param x object to coerce                                 
      229 +/// @param row.names optional row names                       
      230 +/// @return data.frame                                        
      231 +/// @namespace base                                           
      232 +#[builtin(name = "as.data.frame", min_args = 1)]              
      233 +fn builtin_as_data_frame(args: &[RValue], named: &[(String, RV
          +alue)]) -> Result<RValue, RError> {                           
      234 +    match args.first() {                                      
      235 +        Some(RValue::List(list)) => {                         
      236 +            // Already a list ‚ÄĒ add data.frame class if not pr
          +esent                                                         
      237 +            let mut list = list.clone();                      
      238 +            let mut attrs = list.attrs.take().unwrap_or_defaul
          +t();                                                          
      239 +            attrs.insert(                                     
      240 +                "class".to_string(),                          
      241 +                RValue::vec(Vector::Character(                
      242 +                    vec![Some("data.frame".to_string())].into(
          +),                                                            
      243 +                )),                                           
      244 +            );                                                
      245 +            // Add row.names if missing                       
      246 +            if !attrs.contains_key("row.names") {             
      247 +                let nrow = list                               
      248 +                    .values                                   
      249 +                    .first()                                  
      250 +                    .map(|(_, v)| match v {                   
      251 +                        RValue::Vector(rv) => rv.len(),       
      252 +                        _ => 1,                               
      253 +                    })                                        
      254 +                    .unwrap_or(0);                            
      255 +                attrs.insert(                                 
      256 +                    "row.names".to_string(),                  
      257 +                    RValue::vec(Vector::Integer(              
      258 +                        (1..=nrow as i64).map(Some).collect::<
          +Vec<_>>().into(),                                             
      259 +                    )),                                       
      260 +                );                                            
      261 +            }                                                 
      262 +            list.attrs = Some(Box::new(attrs));               
      263 +            Ok(RValue::List(list))                            
      264 +        }                                                     
      265 +        Some(RValue::Vector(v)) => {                          
      266 +            // Single vector ‚Üí single-column data frame       
      267 +            let col_name = named                              
      268 +                .iter()                                       
      269 +                .find(|(n, _)| n == "col.names")              
      270 +                .and_then(|(_, v)| v.as_vector()?.as_character
          +_scalar())                                                    
      271 +                .unwrap_or_else(|| "V1".to_string());         
      272 +            let nrow = v.len();                               
      273 +            let mut list = RList::new(vec![(Some(col_name.clon
          +e()), RValue::Vector(v.clone()))]);                           
      274 +            let mut attrs: IndexMap<String, RValue> = IndexMap
          +::new();                                                      
      275 +            attrs.insert(                                     
      276 +                "class".to_string(),                          
      277 +                RValue::vec(Vector::Character(                
      278 +                    vec![Some("data.frame".to_string())].into(
          +),                                                            
      279 +                )),                                           
      280 +            );                                                
      281 +            attrs.insert(                                     
      282 +                "names".to_string(),                          
      283 +                RValue::vec(Vector::Character(vec![Some(col_na
          +me)].into())),                                                
      284 +            );                                                
      285 +            attrs.insert(                                     
      286 +                "row.names".to_string(),                      
      287 +                RValue::vec(Vector::Integer(                  
      288 +                    (1..=nrow as i64).map(Some).collect::<Vec<
          +_>>().into(),                                                 
      289 +                )),                                           
      290 +            );                                                
      291 +            list.attrs = Some(Box::new(attrs));               
      292 +            Ok(RValue::List(list))                            
      293 +        }                                                     
      294 +        Some(RValue::Null) => {                               
      295 +            let list = RList::new(vec![]);                    
      296 +            let mut attrs: IndexMap<String, RValue> = IndexMap
          +::new();                                                      
      297 +            attrs.insert(                                     
      298 +                "class".to_string(),                          
      299 +                RValue::vec(Vector::Character(                
      300 +                    vec![Some("data.frame".to_string())].into(
          +),                                                            
      301 +                )),                                           
      302 +            );                                                
      303 +            attrs.insert(                                     
      304 +                "row.names".to_string(),                      
      305 +                RValue::vec(Vector::Integer(vec![].into())),  
      306 +            );                                                
      307 +            let mut list = list;                              
      308 +            list.attrs = Some(Box::new(attrs));               
      309 +            Ok(RValue::List(list))                            
      310 +        }                                                     
      311 +        _ => Err(RError::new(                                 
      312 +            RErrorKind::Argument,                             
      313 +            "cannot coerce to data.frame".to_string(),        
      314 +        )),                                                   
      315 +    }                                                         
      316 +}                                                             
      317 +                                                              
      318 +/// Coerce an object to a factor.                             
      319 +///                                                           
      320 +/// @param x object to coerce                                 
      321 +/// @return factor                                            
      322 +/// @namespace base                                           
      323 +#[builtin(name = "as.factor", min_args = 1)]                  
      324 +fn builtin_as_factor(args: &[RValue], _: &[(String, RValue)]) 
          +-> Result<RValue, RError> {                                   
      325 +    // Convert to character first, then create a factor       
      326 +    let chars = match args.first() {                          
      327 +        Some(RValue::Vector(v)) => {                          
      328 +            if is_factor(v) {                                 
      329 +                return Ok(RValue::Vector(v.clone()));         
      330 +            }                                                 
      331 +            v.to_characters()                                 
      332 +        }                                                     
      333 +        _ => vec![],                                          
      334 +    };                                                        
      335 +                                                              
      336 +    // Get unique levels                                      
      337 +    let mut levels: Vec<String> = Vec::new();                 
      338 +    for c in &chars {                                         
      339 +        if let Some(s) = c {                                  
      340 +            if !levels.contains(s) {                          
      341 +                levels.push(s.clone());                       
      342 +            }                                                 
      343 +        }                                                     
      344 +    }                                                         
      345 +    levels.sort();                                            
      346 +                                                              
      347 +    // Map values to integer codes                            
      348 +    let codes: Vec<Option<i64>> = chars                       
      349 +        .iter()                                               
      350 +        .map(|c| {                                            
      351 +            c.as_ref().and_then(|s| {                         
      352 +                levels                                        
      353 +                    .iter()                                   
      354 +                    .position(|l| l == s)                     
      355 +                    .map(|i| (i + 1) as i64)                  
      356 +            })                                                
      357 +        })                                                    
      358 +        .collect();                                           
      359 +                                                              
      360 +    let mut rv = RVector::from(Vector::Integer(codes.into()));
      361 +    rv.set_attr(                                              
      362 +        "levels".to_string(),                                 
      363 +        RValue::vec(Vector::Character(                        
      364 +            levels.into_iter().map(Some).collect::<Vec<_>>().i
          +nto(),                                                        
      365 +        )),                                                   
      366 +    );                                                        
      367 +    rv.set_attr(                                              
      368 +        "class".to_string(),                                  
      369 +        RValue::vec(Vector::Character(                        
      370 +            vec![Some("factor".to_string())].into(),          
      371 +        )),                                                   
      372 +    );                                                        
      373 +    Ok(RValue::Vector(rv))                                    
      374 +}                                                             
      375 +                                                              
      376 +/// Coerce a string to a symbol/name.                         
      377 +///                                                           
      378 +/// @param x character scalar                                 
      379 +/// @return name (Language wrapping Expr::Symbol)             
      380 +/// @namespace base                                           
      381 +#[builtin(name = "as.name", min_args = 1, names = ["as.symbol"
          +])]                                                           
      382 +fn builtin_as_name(args: &[RValue], _: &[(String, RValue)]) ->
          + Result<RValue, RError> {                                     
      383 +    let name = match args.first() {                           
      384 +        Some(RValue::Vector(v)) => v.as_character_scalar().unw
          +rap_or_default(),                                             
      385 +        _ => String::new(),                                   
      386 +    };                                                        
      387 +    Ok(RValue::Language(Language::new(                        
      388 +        crate::parser::ast::Expr::Symbol(name),               
      389 +    )))                                                       
      390 +}                                                             
      391 +                                                              
      392 +/// Look up a function by name or return it if already a funct
          +ion.                                                          
      393 +///                                                           
      394 +/// @param FUN function or character string naming a function 
      395 +/// @return the function                                      
      396 +/// @namespace base                                           
      397 +#[builtin(name = "match.fun", min_args = 1)]                  
      398 +fn builtin_match_fun(args: &[RValue], _: &[(String, RValue)]) 
          +-> Result<RValue, RError> {                                   
      399 +    match args.first() {                                      
      400 +        Some(RValue::Function(_)) => Ok(args[0].clone()),     
      401 +        Some(RValue::Vector(v)) => {                          
      402 +            let name = v.as_character_scalar().ok_or_else(|| {
      403 +                RError::new(                                  
      404 +                    RErrorKind::Argument,                     
      405 +                    "'FUN' must be a function or a character s
          +tring".to_string(),                                           
      406 +                )                                             
      407 +            })?;                                              
      408 +            // Can't do environment lookup from a plain builti
          +n ‚ÄĒ return an error                                           
      409 +            // suggesting the user pass the function directly 
      410 +            Err(RError::new(                                  
      411 +                RErrorKind::Other,                            
      412 +                format!(                                      
      413 +                    "match.fun cannot resolve '{}' ‚ÄĒ pass the 
          +function directly",                                           
      414 +                    name                                      
      415 +                ),                                            
      416 +            ))                                                
      417 +        }                                                     
      418 +        _ => Err(RError::new(                                 
      419 +            RErrorKind::Argument,                             
      420 +            "'FUN' must be a function or a character string".t
          +o_string(),                                                   
      421 +        )),                                                   
      422 +    }                                                         
      423 +}                                                             
      424 +                                                              
      425  /// Coerce an object to a vector, stripping all attributes.
      426  ///
      427  /// @param x object to coerce
